web/modules/custom/ilas_site_assistant/ILAS_ASSISTANT_REPORT.md:31:The `ilas_site_assistant` module is a custom Drupal chatbot for Idaho Legal Aid Services (ILAS). It helps users find FAQs, legal resources, forms, and guides — and directs them to apply for help or call the Legal Advice Line — **without providing legal advice**.
web/modules/custom/ilas_site_assistant/ILAS_ASSISTANT_REPORT.md:35:A client-side JavaScript widget (or dedicated `/assistant` page) sends user messages via POST to `/assistant/api/message`. The controller runs a 32-step processing pipeline: rate-limit → safety classification → out-of-scope detection → policy filter → intent routing (deterministic, rule-based NLP) → FAQ/resource retrieval → fallback gate → optional LLM enhancement → canonical URL enforcement → response grounding → analytics logging. Every response is a structured JSON contract with a `type`, `message`, `primary_action` URL, and optional `results`.
